[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in Wireshark's ICMP packet [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissector during fuzzing with AddressSanitizer. The issue occurs when processing [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissection. The vulnerability involves a [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m-byte write operation that overflows a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack-allocated buffer, with a SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m indicating a [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmulti-byte-write-stack-buffer-overflow.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability, specifically a write operation that [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempts to copy [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m bytes to a memory location on the stack that does not have [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msufficient space allocated.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests during the execution of the `handler_icmp` fuzzer when [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing a test case. The AddressSanitizer detected a WRITE of [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m bytes at [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddress `[0m[1;36m0x7f513d381aa0[0m[39m`, which is beyond the bounds of allocated stack memory.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Call Stack Analysis[0m                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1040[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Add a subtree for this object [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe text will be reset later[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1041[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39mext_object_tree = [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_subtree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mext_tree, tvb, offset,[0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1043[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39mett_icmp_ext_object, &tf_object, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"Unknown object"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1044[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1045[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_uint[0m[1;39m([0m[39mext_object_tree, hf_icmp_ext_length,[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1046[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m    tvb, offset, [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m, obj_length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1047[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1048[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Class *[0m[35m/[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1049[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39mclass_num = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset + [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1050[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mext_object_tree, hf_icmp_ext_class,[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1051[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m    tvb, offset + [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, ENC_BIG_ENDIAN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1052[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1053[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* C-Type *[0m[35m/[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1054[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39mc_type = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset + [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1056[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mobj_length < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Object header *[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1057[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Thanks doc/README.developer :[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1058[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mproto_item_set_text[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtf_object,[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1059[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m    [0m[32m"Object with bad length"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1060[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39mbreak;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1061[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1062[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1063[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1064[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39mswitch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mclass_num[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1065[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39mcase MPLS_STACK_ENTRY_OBJECT_CLASS:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Core Issues Identified[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Primary Vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m927[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: The function [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_interface_identification_object` performs an unbounded `tvb_memcpy` into a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m128[0m[39m-byte stack buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ident_name`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without validating that `obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdoesn't exceed `ICMP_MAX_IDENT_NAME_LENGTH`.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Secondary Issue [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m929[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m931[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: The printability check loop iterates [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` times, which can exceed buffer bounds and is effectively dead code[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mthe loop breaks on first non-printable character but doesn't use the result[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Redundant Buffer**: The `ident_name` buffer at line [0m[1;36m902[0m[39m is only used for the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdead code printability check. Line [0m[1;36m933[0m[39m displays the data by reading directly from [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe TVB, making the intermediate buffer unnecessary.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe function reads `obj_length` from the network packet at line [0m[1;36m909[0m[39m without [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidating it against `ICMP_MAX_IDENT_NAME_LENGTH` before using it in the [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tvb_memcpy` call at line [0m[1;36m927[0m[39m. An attacker can craft a packet with `obj_length = [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m260[0m[39m`, causing `obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m` bytes to be copied into a [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m-byte buffer, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresulting in a stack buffer overflow.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Existing Codebase Patterns[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAnalysis of similar functions shows the standard pattern used throughout the file:[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. `dissect_mpls_extended_payload_object` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m625[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m663[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. `dissect_mpls_stack_entry_object` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m665[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m762[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. `dissect_interface_information_object` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m765[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m891[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAll three functions:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Calculate `obj_trunc_length = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mobj_length, [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Use `proto_tree_add_item` directly from TVB without intermediate buffers[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Perform bounds checking before accessing data[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Approach: Minimal Change with Bounds Checking[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mGiven that the printability check [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m929[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m931[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is dead code that doesn't affect [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality, and line [0m[1;36m933[0m[39m already displays the data correctly using [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`proto_tree_add_item` directly from the TVB, the optimal fix is to:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Add bounds checking before `tvb_memcpy`** at line [0m[1;36m927[0m[39m to prevent buffer [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Apply the same bounds to the printability check loop** at line [0m[1;36m929[0m[39m to prevent [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout-of-bounds reads[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Preserve the existing logic** to avoid breaking any potential future use of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe printability check[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Steps[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `epan/dissectors/packet-icmp.c`, function [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_interface_identification_object`, lines [0m[1;36m925[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m934[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes Required**:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Before line [0m[1;36m927[0m[39m, calculate a safe copy length:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   uint16_t name_length = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mobj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, ICMP_MAX_IDENT_NAME_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Replace line [0m[1;36m927[0m[39m to use the bounded length:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, ident_name, offset, name_length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Replace line [0m[1;36m929[0m[39m to use the bounded length:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   for [0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < name_length; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Keep line [0m[1;36m933[0m[39m unchanged [0m[1;39m([0m[39mit already uses `obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` correctly with TVB [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich handles its own bounds[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mext_object_tree, hf_icmp_int_ident_name_string, tvb, offset,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mobj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, ENC_ASCII[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Complete Patched Code Section[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe ICMP_EXT_ECHO_IDENT_NAME case [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m925[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m934[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m should be modified as follows:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcase ICMP_EXT_ECHO_IDENT_NAME:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Identification Name must be printable*[0m[35m/[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        uint16_t name_length = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mobj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, ICMP_MAX_IDENT_NAME_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, ident_name, offset, name_length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        for [0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < name_length; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mg_ascii_isprint[0m[1;39m([0m[39mident_name[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                break;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mext_object_tree, hf_icmp_int_ident_name_string, tvb, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset, obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, ENC_ASCII[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    break;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Code Changes**: Only adds bounds checking without restructuring the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Follows Existing Patterns**: Uses the same [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m macro pattern found in lines [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m638[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m639[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m684[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m685[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m787[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m788[0m[39m, and [0m[1;36m1034[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1036[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Preserves Functionality**: Maintains the printability check loop for potential[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuture use[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes**: Doesn't modify the display logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m933[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which works[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Maintains RFC [0m[1;36m8335[0m[39m Compliance**: Enforces the ICMP_MAX_IDENT_NAME_LENGTH limit[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas intended[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issues[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Prevents Stack Buffer Overflow**: The [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m macro ensures `name_length` never [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceeds [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m bytes[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Prevents Out-of-Bounds Reads**: The loop at line [0m[1;36m929[0m[39m now iterates only [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`name_length` times[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Maintains Correct Display**: Line [0m[1;36m933[0m[39m still displays the full data from TVB [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mup to `obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, even if we only copied part of it to the buffer for [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Preserved Logic[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Display Functionality**: The proto_tree_add_item call still displays the full [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minterface name from the packet[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Printability Check**: Still performed on the portion that fits in the buffer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mthough the result isn't currently used[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Other Case Statements**: No changes to ICMP_EXT_ECHO_IDENT_INDEX and [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mICMP_EXT_ECHO_IDENT_ADDRESS cases[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Parent Function Flow**: No changes to dissect_icmp_extension or other callers[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigations[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Truncation of Printability Check**: If a name longer than [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m bytes is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreceived, only the first [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m bytes are checked for printability. This is acceptable[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbecause:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The check result isn't currently used for validation or warning[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The full name is still displayed to the user via line [0m[1;36m933[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The ICMP_MAX_IDENT_NAME_LENGTH constant indicates [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m bytes is the intended [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaximum[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **No Impact on Display**: The proto_tree_add_item at line [0m[1;36m933[0m[39m reads directly [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom the TVB with `obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`, so the full interface name [0m[1;39m([0m[39msubject to TVB's [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mown bounds checking[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is still displayed regardless of the buffer limitation.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Consistency with Codebase[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix aligns with similar bounds checking patterns found throughout [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpacket-icmp.c:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m638[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m639[0m[39m: `obj_trunc_length = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mobj_length, [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m684[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m685[0m[39m: Same pattern[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m787[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m788[0m[39m: Same pattern  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m1034[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1036[0m[39m: Same pattern[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe use of [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for bounds checking is the established pattern in this file.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
